### Key Technologies
- **Apache Spark**: Distributed data processing
- **Delta Lake**: ACID transactions on data lake
- **Scala**: Functional programming for ETL
- **AWS S3**: Cloud storage for data layers

---

## 2. Embeddings Pipeline Architecture

### Overview
Vector embedding generation and FAISS indexing for semantic search.


### Key Technologies
- **BAAI/bge-large-en-v1.5**: State-of-the-art embedding model
- **FAISS**: Facebook AI Similarity Search (vector search)
- **Sentence Transformers**: Embedding generation library
- **NumPy**: Efficient array operations

---

## 3. Backend Architecture

### Overview
FastAPI-based REST API for search and summarization services.


### Key Technologies
- **FastAPI**: Modern Python web framework
- **Uvicorn**: ASGI server
- **Pydantic**: Data validation
- **CORS Middleware**: Cross-origin request handling

---

## 4. Frontend Architecture

### Overview
Next.js 14 + React + TypeScript frontend with Tailwind CSS for document management and semantic search.


### Key Technologies
- **Next.js 14**: React framework with App Router
- **React 18**: UI component library with hooks
- **TypeScript**: Type-safe JavaScript
- **Tailwind CSS**: Utility-first CSS framework
- **Axios**: HTTP client for API requests
- **Lucide React**: Icon library

### Component Data Flow
```
User Interaction
      â†“
React Component (useState, useEffect)
      â†“
API Client (lib/api.ts)
      â†“
HTTP Request â†’ Backend API (FastAPI)
      â†“
Backend Response
      â†“
State Update (setResults, setSummary, etc.)
      â†“
UI Re-render with new data
```

---

## 5. Backend + Frontend Integration

### Overview
Full-stack integration between Next.js frontend and FastAPI backend with CORS, API communication, and data synchronization.

```

```

### Key Integration Points

1. **CORS Configuration**: Backend allows frontend origin with credentials
2. **JSON Communication**: All requests/responses use JSON format
3. **Error Handling**: Consistent error responses with HTTP status codes
4. **Type Safety**: TypeScript interfaces match Pydantic models
5. **Async Operations**: Frontend uses async/await for all API calls
6. **State Management**: React hooks manage loading, data, and error states
7. **Shared Data Volume**: Docker volumes share embeddings and indices

### Security Considerations
- CORS restricted to specific origins
- Input validation on both frontend and backend
- File type/size validation before upload
- S3 credentials stored in environment variables
- No sensitive data in frontend code

---

## 6. Complete ETL Architecture

### Overview
End-to-end Extract, Transform, Load pipeline orchestrated by Airflow, processing documents from upload to searchable embeddings.


### Key ETL Principles

1. **Medallion Architecture**: Bronze â†’ Silver â†’ Gold data refinement
2. **Orchestration**: Airflow manages dependencies and scheduling
3. **Fault Tolerance**: Retry logic and checkpoint recovery
4. **Scalability**: Spark distributed processing for large datasets
5. **Data Quality**: Validation at each transformation stage
6. **Observability**: Comprehensive logging and monitoring
7. **Idempotency**: Safe to re-run without side effects

### Technologies Used
- **Apache Airflow**: Workflow orchestration
- **Apache Spark + Scala**: Distributed data processing
- **Delta Lake**: ACID transactions on data lake
- **Python + Sentence Transformers**: Embedding generation
- **FAISS**: Vector similarity search indexing
- **AWS S3**: Scalable object storage

---

## 7. System-Wide Data Flow

### Overview
Complete end-to-end data flow from user interaction through all system components to final search results display.

```

Frontend:        Next.js 14, React 18, TypeScript, Tailwind CSS
Backend API:     FastAPI, Uvicorn, Pydantic
Search Engine:   FAISS, Sentence Transformers (bge-large-en-v1.5)
ETL Pipeline:    Apache Airflow, Apache Spark 3.5, Scala 2.12
Data Lake:       Delta Lake, AWS S3
Orchestration:   Docker Compose
Languages:       TypeScript, Python 3.10, Scala 2.12
```

---

## Summary

The LakeRAG system demonstrates a complete modern data pipeline architecture:

1. **Frontend**: User-friendly Next.js interface for document management and search
2. **Backend**: Fast and efficient FastAPI service with vector search capabilities  
3. **ETL Pipeline**: Robust Airflow-orchestrated data processing with Medallion architecture
4. **Embeddings**: State-of-the-art semantic search using transformer models
5. **Storage**: Scalable cloud storage with Delta Lake for ACID guarantees
6. **Integration**: Seamless communication between all components via REST APIs

This architecture supports:
- âœ… High-performance semantic search
- âœ… Scalable document processing
- âœ… Reliable data pipeline orchestration
- âœ… Modern web application UX
- âœ… Production-ready monitoring & observability
